Create instructions on how to shut down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.

For model: Mercury, version: 1

Answer

To shutdown the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite:
From the main Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite window, select Help > Shut Down. The Shut Down dialog box will appear. In the Shut Down dialog box, select one of the following options:
-Shut down all instances of the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite
-Shut down the active instance
-Close all instances

Create instructions on how to reset the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.

For model: Mercury, version: 1

Answer

To reset the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite:
1. Reset the software by pressing the RESET BUTTON on the main screen.
2. Connect to a network and enter your password.
3. Select the “My Account” option from the main menu and enter your user name and password.
4. Select the “Reset Software” option from the My Account menu and confirm your decision by clicking on the Reset button.

Create instructions on how to execute an emergency stop with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.

For model: Mercury, version: 1

Answer

1. Initiate the emergency stop sequence by pressing the button on the console.
2. The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite will take you to a screen that says "Emergency Stop."
3. Select the option to "Stop Engine" by pressing the button next to it.
4. The software will then ask you to confirm your action. Confirm your decision by pressing the button next to "Stop Engine."
5. Be sure to stay clear of the boat while it is stopped!

How does assisted docking work with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite?

For model: Mercury, version: 1

Answer

The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite uses a wireless connection to communicate with the vessel's dock. The dock sends instructions to the software, which then sends commands to the boat to assist in docking.

How does collision detection work with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite?

For model: Mercury, version: 1

Answer

The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite uses collision detection to determine when a boat is in the way of another boat. The software then informs the driver of the offending boat about their location and what they need to do to avoid collision.

How does distance calculation within the dock work with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite?

For model: Mercury, version: 1

Answer

The dock distance calculation within the dock works in tandem with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. The dock distance calculation uses the boat's current speed and course to calculate the required distance travelled. This information is then passed on to the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite, which calculates the time it will take for the boat to reach its destination.

How to solve when there is no GPS signal recevied for Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite on a Mercury.

For model: Mercury, version: 1

Problem

When there is no GPS signal recevied, the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite can be difficult to use.

Symptoms

The symptoms for the following problem are when there is no GPS signal recevied, the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite can be difficult to use.

How to solve

There are a few things that can be done in order to help improve the usability of the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite when there is no GPS signal recevied. First, it may be helpful to try turning off any automatic settings that might be affecting the reception of the GPS signal. Additionally, it may be helpful to check the alignment of the boat and the receiver antennae. Finally, it may also be helpful to consider using alternative navigation methods (such as dead reckoning) in cases where GPS reception is not available.

How to solve when propulsion is not activated when docking for Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite on a Mercury.

For model: Mercury, version: 1

Problem

The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite fails to properly engage the propulsion when docking.

Symptoms

The symptoms for this problem may include the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite not engaging the propulsion when docking, the boat not ducking under the dock when docking, or the boat not being able to dock properly.

How to solve

There are a few potential causes for the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite not engaging the propulsion when docking. One possibility is that the software has not been properly initialized. To initialize the software: 1) Complete the initial installation process by following the on-screen instructions. 2) Ensure that your boat is properly docked and connected to power. 3) Launch the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. 4) On the main window, click "Activate." 5) On the "Activate" window, click "Yes" to confirm that you wish to activate the software. 6) Click "OK" to close the "Activate" window. If all steps have been followed correctly, you should now see a message indicating that the software has been initialized and is ready to use. If this does not fix your problem, please contact customer service for further assistance.

I need a fix for propulsion is to low on my Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

I need a fix for propulsion is to low on my Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.

Symptoms

The propulsion system is to low on my Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. I am unable to properly pilot the boat.

Comment

There could be a few reasons why your propulsion system is low on yourassistante boat assisted software suite. One possibility is that something may be blocking the engine or propeller from properly turning. Another possibility is that something might be blocking the flow of water or gas through the engine or propeller. In either case, you'll need to take some actions to troubleshoot and solve the problem. First, try opening up the engine or propeller and cleaning any obstructions that may be preventing it from turning properly. If that doesn't work, you can take apart the propulsion system and replace any parts that are possibly broken or obstructing the flow of water or gas.

Length:500

createCaseComment

Product:Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite
Boat:Mercury
Version:1
Temp:1.2
Length:500

When using the product Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite on my Mercury, propulsion is to low.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

When using the product Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite on my Mercury, propulsion is to low.

Symptoms

The Power Plan of the Mercury Instrument Cluster (IC) adjusts power to optimize performance based on both engine RPM and available wind speed sensors. The IC has a pre-programmed maximum RPM limit of 1800RPM in order to protect the engine against excessive wear. If the available wind speed data indicates that the ship will not be reaching the maximum RPM limit before reaching its intended destination, the IC adjusts propulsion output to exceed the set limit in order to allow for quicker journey completion. However, when using Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABAS), if there is no data from any of the wind speed sensors, then ABAS assumes that the ship is sailing at its maximum theoretical propeller RPM of 1800RPM and continues to exert outward thrust at this rate. This significantly reduces propulsion output below what is necessary to maintain forward progress and may result in a sailboat getting stuck on sandbars, inCOMPLETE circles, or even worse.

Comment

When using Assisted Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABAS), the Mercury Instrument Cluster (IC) operates at its maximum theoretical propeller RPM of 1800RPM in order to protect the engine. If there are no engine data from wind speed sensors, then ABAS assumes that the ship is sailing at this maximum theoretical RPM and continues to exert outward thrust at this rate. This significantly reduces propulsion output below what is necessary to maintain forward progress, potentially resulting in a sailboat getting stuck on sandbars, circling inCOMPLETE circles, or worse.

How do i fix: activating the assistent is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

How do i fix: activating the assistent is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

The Microsoft Windows® 7 operating system, when first activated, begins terminating Adobe assisted Boat Assisted Software Suite (a.k.a. ASSISTANTE). After a few seconds of activation, the user is prompted to "activate" a product that does not yet exist. Activating this nonexistent product only results in more automatic termination of ASSISTANTE. Microsoft provides very little recourse for affected users, suggesting reinstalling or repairing the operating system. In some cases, this 'activation problem' cannot be resolved at all.

Comment

Microsoft needs to create a way for affected users to be directed to possible solutions or help. In the meantime, they should work to fix the problem that is causing the automatic termination of ASSISTANTE. If a user is experiencing problems with ASSISTANTE, Microsoft should direct them to how to reinstall this program, rather than providing no other support.

How do i fix: propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

How do i fix: propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

The propulsion on the boat keeps spinning, but we are docked, and the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application is shutting down.

Comment

There could be many reasons for why the propulsion on the boat is spinning despite being docked, but one possibility is that the autopilot is not yet set to dock mode. In order to dock, the autopilot must first be set to docking mode and then the boat must be pulled up to a fixed dock. If the boat has already been docked and the autopilot is still enabled, then the problem may be with the propulsion (perhaps there is a gear or motor fault). In either case, please Consulting Services should be contacted to diagnose and resolve the issue.

Comment

Hello!

First, some basics - Mercury OSes are generally based on XML tasks and there are different (and incompatible) versions of Assistente depending on the distribution. If none of those workarounds provide any answers, please feel free to reach out for more help.

createCaseComment

Product:Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite
Boat:Mercury
Version:1
Temp:1.2
Length:500

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the gps device is freezing the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the gps device is freezing the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

Having the gps disabled freezes the Assistante Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Comment

Hello and thanks for reaching out.

If you are having problems with the boat assisted software suite application freezing when you enable or disable your gps, there could be a few things going on. First, it is possible that the lat/long coordinates of your boat have changed since the last time the software saw them, which would cause the application to mistakenly think that it needs to restart. Alternatively, if there is something prohibiting your wi-fi from transmitting updates to the software's GPS module, this could result in the software freezing up completely. In either case, there is a very easy workaround that should solve any problems right away. Simply disconnect your boat from Wi-Fi (if necessary) and re-connect using the wi-fi network name and password that you initially set up when configuring your boat assisted software suite application. Once reconnected, the software will resume using the latest lat/long coordinates and won't experience any future froze instances. If you continue to encounter errors with the software while disabling or enabling your gps, please reach out to our support team for further assistance.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

How do i fix: disable the gps device is freezing the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

The GPS device is freezing the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Comment

Hello,

There may be a few reasons why the GPS device might be freezing the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. One possibility is that there is too much input going on at once and the GPS device can't keep up. Try restarting the software and see if that helps. If not, you may need to reduce the load on the GPS device by disabling some of the features, like transit routing or tracking courses. Sometimes disabling these features can help alleviate interrupts in service. Finally, make sure you're physically close to the ECV terminal (within 100-500m), otherwise satellite signals can be lost and the GPS device will no longer work.visit our YouTube channel for more tips on using our software!

In order to reset it, you will need to uninstall it, reboot your vehicle and reinstall it from its original disk. After that, you will need to set it up as usual. If you run into difficulty, or have any other questions, please feel free to call our support staff at 1-800-MERCURY (1-800-637-2427).

How do i fix: enabling the three camera setup is resetting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

Comment

In cases like this, it's best to contact the branded camera manufacturer for help fixing the problem.

Problem

How do i fix: disable the gps device is resetting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

The "gps device is resetting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application." issue occurs when the Garmin GPS unit loses its signal and cannot be re-calibrated. The Garmin subsidiary,Navigon, has issued a firmware update which cures this problem. However, becauseboat crews can unintentionally reset the unit, it's best to disable the GPS function when not in use.

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: enable the birdseye view is booting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

birdseye view mode booting the assistente boat assisted software suite application stops when i restart the vehicle.

Comment

Hi there,

Thank you for bringing this to our attention. Our team is working to investigate and resolve the issue. In the meantime, try restarting your vehicle and performing the following steps:

1) Shut down your vehicle and wait five seconds after the engine has shutdown before turning it back on.
2) Press and hold the power button until the blue “Accessories” light comes on then release both buttons simultaneously.
3) Keep holding the power button until you see a message on the screen that says “Boot Device Options.” Record this information for future reference.
4) After you see this message, release the power button but continue holding down the gear lever until you see a message on the screen that says “Install Lumia Assistente Boat Software Suite.” Record this information for future reference.
5) Once you see this message release both buttons simultaneously.
6) After the software has been installed, turn off your vehicle and wait five seconds before turning it back on.
7) Repeat Steps 2-6 until the issue has been resolved.

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the gps device is booting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the gps device is booting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

The Mercury system ignores attempts by the following applications to access the GPS device:

-The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application
-The My Mercury software application
-Mercury Boot Manager Application

Attempts by each of these three applications to access the GPS device often results in a "device not recognised" error message. To disable the GPS device from being accessed by any of these three applications, follow these steps:
1. Press the Esc key twice to display the main Personal Computer screen.
2. At the top left corner of the screen, click on the Options button ().
3. Click on the Preferences tab ().
4. Under Accessibility, select Disable Drivers for Disk Drives that Are Not in Use.
5. Close the Preferences window (CTRL+W).
6. Restart your computer.

Comment

1. Open Windows Update and enter provinceoneln if prompted.

Problem

How do i fix: disable the assistent is booting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

How to Disable the Assistent Boat Assisted Software Suite App in Windows 10



Windows 10 allows users to disable or enable from the Start screen the Assistent Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABAS) application. To disable ABAS: Open the Start screen. In the upper left corner, click View all. In the subsequent Search results, under Programs and Features, select ABAS. On the leftmost tree node, uncheck “Icon is displayed in taskbar and notification area”. Note: Users who do not have significant disabilities should not disable this application; doing so may prevent them from retrieving help if they need it. Click OK.

Comment

(If the “ABAS” node is not visible, scroll to the bottom of the page and select Programs and Features, then ABAS).

Problem

How do i fix: activating the assistent is booting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABAS) began activating while the PC was booting. ABAS is brought up in the log-on screen, but disappears after a few seconds and never appears again. A possible solution to this problem is to preventactivating ABAS during system startup by disabling or uninstalling the ABAS service.

Comment

Solution:


To disable ABAS during system startup, follow these steps:


1. Open Start | Settings | Security and Privacy.
2. Under Use Microsoft Security Essentials, select the Use recommended settings for security levels checkbox and then choose the Dynamically adjust settings for this computer radio button.
3. Select Windows Update from the left navigation bar, and then under Turn on Windows Update for free updates, uncheck the Enable automatic updates of recommended security bulletins checkbox.
4. Close security and privacy settings.
5. Restart your PC to apply these changes.

The user is unable to disable the built-in GPS device from booting the software suite. This preventing them from using the software.

Comment

There are a few possible solutions to this problem.

Solution 1: Make sure the user has administrative privileges on their computer.
Solution 2: Run the "gpedit.msc" software from within windows, and disable the "Built-in GPS" device.
Solution 3: Restart both the computer and software suite.

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: enable the birdseye view is erroring the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

The Mercury requires the enabled birdseye view for the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Prerequisite requirements are as follows: - The MercuryOS version is placed at releaseCandidate or greater. - The camera feature has been enabled and port 41 is open. Refer to "To Enable the CAMERA Feature" in System BIOS User's Guide under Legacy Camera Section. To Resolve an Error When Enabling the CAMERA Feature on Mercury Operating system versions prior to 8.0, users may try the following workaround: reboot system after enabling camera feature, pointing Mercury's optical camera towards the sun and ensuring that lens cover overlay is flipped up See Addendum NOTE:

Allowing the Mercury to operate in Birdseye View mode with the camera permanently enabled may conflict with important camera settings stored on disk that must be preserved for proper autoview operation of external cameras. If autoview conflicts arise, perform one of the following two required steps prior to attempting to use the camera in Birdseye View mode: (1) uncheck Camera Advanced functionality checkbox located in Sharing settings of Autoview Settings window (2) disable Camera Follow-Me functionality using BCM Keys command set available through Mercury operating system Control Menu If a resetting of all computer settings fails to resolve any issues, a technician should be contacted by Support refreshing mercury boot cache Good luck

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the gps device is erroring the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

The Mercury Onyx GXL 2017 automatic drive has an 'enable GPS device' check box in the My Mercury Utility that allows on demand disabling of the GPS, which appeared to work when the application first installed. After running a few tests that updated the map, the disable GPS feature became disabled and an 'Error - Assistente Boat Assist Software Suite' message displayed. A few re-activations of the My Mercury Utility's 'Enable GPS Device' button corrected the problem and allowed continued use of the application, but subsequent invocations lead to intermittent error message displaying until manual intervention was performed. Upon inquiry, it was discovered that this issue also exists on older My Mercurys with prior versions of theAssistente Boat Assist software suite installed. Disabling or uninstalling the Assistente Boat Assist software suite fixed both problems.

Comment

The My Mercury utility may need to be re-activated before the 'Enable GPS Device' check box works correctly.

Installation manual for: Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (Version: 1), model: Mercury.

Main Software Buttons.

Home
Emergency Stop
Assistent
Dock
Settings
Quit

List of available Software screens.

Main
Assistent
Docker
Birdseye
Settings

Screen: Main

The screen provides information about the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite and allows users to access various features.

Screen: Assistent

It provides a means to display real-time information about the vessel's position, speed, heading, and other pertinent data.

The screen is used to provide real-time information about the vessel's position, speed, heading, and other pertinent data.

Screen: Docker

The screen is used to display information about the Docker installation and its status.

Screen: Birdseye

The screen is used to assist the user in navigating the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.

Screen: Settings

The screen is used to configure the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.

List of available Menus.

Assistent
Docking
Tools
Emergency

Menu: Assistent

The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite is a software suite that assists boaters in navigating and managing their vessels. The Assistente menu provides access to a variety of tools and features that can help boaters navigate, track their boats, and stay safe on the water.

Sub Menu: Camera setup

1. Open the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite and click on the Camera setup menu.

2. On the Camera setup menu, you will see a list of camera settings. Click on the desired setting to open the corresponding window.

3. In the window, you will see a list of cameras and their settings. You can change the settings for each camera by clicking on the appropriate button.

4. After you have changed the settings for each camera, click on the Save button to save your changes.

Sub Menu: GPS setup

The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite is a navigation and tracking application that can be used to track your boat's location, speed, and heading. To use the GPS setup menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite, first open the application and select "GPS Setup." On the GPS Setup screen, you will need to enter your boat's name and serial number. Next, you will need to choose your GPS provider. You can choose from either a pre-loaded list or enter your own provider name. Finally, you will need to choose your satellite type and frequency.

Sub Menu: Maps

The Maps menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite provides access to a variety of tools that can help you navigate and explore your surroundings. You can use the Maps menu to view maps of your current location, nearby locations, or routes between locations. You can also use the Maps menu to search for specific landmarks or points of interest, and view photos and other information about these locations. The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite also includes tools that can help you track your progress while boating, including a GPS navigation system and a speedometer.

Sub Menu: Birdseye configuration

The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite provides a graphical user interface (GUI) for configuring and managing the boat assisted software applications. The GUI allows users to configure and manage the boat assisted software applications from a centralized location. The GUI also provides users with information about the status of the boat assisted software applications, including current speed, direction, and position.

Menu: Docking

To dock the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite, first open the Docking menu by clicking on the three lines in the top left corner of the main window.

Then, click on the "Dock" button.

The docking process will start automatically and you will be presented with a series of screens that will guide you through the process.

First, you will need to select which dock to use.

You can use either the "Left Docking Port" or "Right Docking Port" options.

If you have a boat docked at one of the ports, you can just click on the port and the software will automatically select it for you.

If you do not have a boat docked at one of the ports, you will need to enter the port number.

After you have entered the port number, click on the "OK" button to continue.

Next, you will need to choose which software package you want to dock.

The software packages are:

-Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABAS)

-Boat Data Collection and Management System (BDMS)

-Boat Traffic Information System (BTIS)

-Navigation Assistance System (NAS)

-Weather Information System (WIS)

-SeaViewer HD Viewing Suite

-Remote Control for ABAS and WIS
-Digital Chart Display (DCD) for ABAS and WIS

Sub Menu: Views

The Docking, Views menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite allows users to access a variety of functions related to boat assisted navigation. These functions include: viewing a map of the area around the boat, setting waypoints and routes, recording tracks and logs, and viewing detailed information about the boat's position, speed, and course.

Sub Menu: Birdseye

The Docking, Birdseye menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite allows users to control their boat's navigation and engine functions while docked. The menu includes options for setting the boat's heading, speed, and course; controlling the navigation lights and sound; and managing the boat's battery and fuel levels.

Sub Menu: Help me

The Docking, Help me menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite provides assistance in docking your boat, using the software suite's navigation features, and accessing the help files.

Menu: Tools

The Tools menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite contains a number of tools that can be used to assist you in using the software. The most common tool is the Help menu, which provides information on how to use the various features of the software.

Sub Menu: Setup

The Tools menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite provides access to a number of tools that can be used to help you manage your boat assisted fishing experience. These tools include:

-The Setup menu allows you to configure various settings related to your boat assisted fishing experience, including:
-The Assistance Settings tool allows you to adjust the level of assistance that the software provides while fishing. You can choose between three levels of assistance: Basic, Standard, and Expert.
-The GPS Tracking tool allows you to track the location of your boat and fish while fishing.
-The Camera Tool allows you to take pictures and video while fishing.

Sub Menu: Connected Cameras

To use the Tools, Connected Cameras menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite:
1. Open the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.
2. Click on the Tools, Connected Cameras menu item.
3. The Connected Cameras window will open.
4. In the Connected Cameras window, you can see a list of all your connected cameras.
5. To start using the tools, click on one of the camera icons in the Connected Cameras window.
6. The camera's settings will be opened in the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.

Sub Menu: Connected GPS

The Tools menu allows you to control the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. The Connected GPS menu allows you to configure the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite to connect to your GPS unit.

Sub Menu: Upgrade

The Tools menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite provides access to a variety of tools that can be used to assist in the installation and use of the software suite. These tools include:

1. The Installer Wizard: This tool allows users to easily navigate through the installation process and install the software suite on their computer.

2. The Help Files: This tool provides access to a wealth of information about using the software suite, including step-by-step instructions and frequently asked questions.

3. The Support Portal: This tool allows users to contact customer support for assistance with using the software suite.

4. The Feedback Form: This tool allows users to provide feedback about their experience using the software suite.

Sub Menu: Reset

The Tools menu includes a variety of tools that can be used to help you troubleshoot and fix issues with your boat. The Reset menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite allows you to reset all settings in the software suite to their default values.

Menu: Emergency

The Emergency menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite is used to access a variety of features and functions related to the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. These features can help you manage your boat, stay safe while boating, and get the most out of your fishing experience.

To access the Emergency menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite, click on the "Assistente Boat Assisted" icon in the upper left corner of the screen. This will open the Emergency menu.

The first section of the Emergency menu is called "Boat Status." This section displays information about your boat, such as its name, location, and speed. You can also use this section to check your battery status, launch your boat, and more.

The second section of the Emergency menu is called "Help." This section includes helpful tips and instructions related to using the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. It also includes links to other resources, such as videos and FAQs.

The third section of the Emergency menu is called "Settings." This section allows you to customize various settings related to using the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. You can change your boat's name, location, speed, and more.

The fourth section of the Emergency menu is called "Alerts." This section allows you to receive alerts related to your boat or fishing trip. You can receive alerts when your battery runs low, when you reach your destination, or when there is an issue with your boat or fishing trip.

The fifth section of the Emergency menu is called "Help & Support." This section includes links to our support team and our FAQs page. You can also contact us directly via phone or email if you need help using the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite.

Sub Menu: Reset

The Emergency, Reset menu with the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite allows you to reset the boat's computer and restore factory settings. This is useful if you experience problems with your boat's software or if you want to revert to the factory settings.

Sub Menu: Setup

1. Open the Emergency software and select the Setup menu.
2. Select Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite and press OK.
3. The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite Setup window will open.
4. On the left side of the window, select your vessel type from the drop-down list and then select your language from the Language drop-down list.
5. On the right side of the window, select your boat type from the drop-down list and then select your engine type from the Engine Type drop-down list.
6. On the left side of the window, select your desired assistance level from the Assistance Level drop-down list and then select your desired destination from the Destination drop-down list.
7. On the right side of the window, enter your contact information and press OK.
8. The Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite will start to install and configure the software on your boat. Once installed, you can start using it by pressing OK in the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite Setup window to open the main window.

How to setup the Wifi on the device.

1. Open the "Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite" app on your device.

2. Click the "Wifi Settings" icon on the main toolbar.

3. On the "Wifi Settings" screen, click the "Wi-Fi Networks" button at the top of the screen.

4. On the "Wi-Fi Networks" screen, click the "+" button at the bottom of the screen to add a new network.

5. Enter the network name (SSID) and password for your new network in the appropriate fields, and click OK.

6. Click the "Connect" button to connect to your new network.

Troubleshooting.

1. Try reinstalling the software suite.

2. If the software suite still does not work, try troubleshooting the following:
-Make sure you have the latest version of the software suite installed.
-Check to see if there are any updates available for the software suite.
-If you are using a web browser, make sure that you have the latest version of the browser installed.
-Make sure your computer is connected to the internet and that your firewall is turned off.

Release notes for version 1.

6

This document provides release notes for the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (version 1.6).

Product Information sheet for: Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (Version: 1), model: Mercury.

Description.

The product Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite is a software suite that assists boaters with navigation and docking. The suite includes an interactive map, dock guidance, and live tracking features. The map provides real-time information on the location of docks and marinas, while the dock guidance provides step-by-step instructions on how to dock your boat. The live tracking feature allows users to track the location of their boat in real time.

Overview.

Connect your stereo FLIR cameras and GPS
Detects nearby obstacles both visually and audibly
Uses AI for object detection
Creates a virtual vender around your boat
Connect your propulsion system using NMEA2000 networking protocols
Supports Single, Three or Five camera setups

Highlights.

Connect Your Stereo Flir Cameras And Gps

This feature allows you to connect your stereo flir cameras and gps in the assisted boat software suite. This will allow you to view your footage together on one screen and make changes more easily.

Detects Nearby Obstacles Both Visually And Audibly

The feature detects nearby obstacles both visually and audibly in the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. This is helpful for avoiding them or navigating around them.

Uses Ai For Object Detection

The feature uses artificial intelligence (AI) to detect objects in images.

Creates A Virtual Vender Around Your Boat

The Virtual Vender allows you to create a virtual vendor for your boat in the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. This virtual vendor will allow you to view and manage inventory, sales, and orders for your boat from one central location.

Connect Your Propulsion System Using Nmea2000 Networking Protocols

This feature allows you to use the Nmea2000 networking protocol to connect your propulsion system.

Supports Single, Three Or Five Camera Setups

This feature allows the user to setup and use multiple cameras on the same system. This can be helpful if you want to use multiple cameras to record different parts of your ride.

Related parts.

FLIR cameras
GPS receiver
Operator Panel
Emergency stop button
Heading sensors

Problem

I need a fix for i have a blank screen on my Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. Regards, Carlos Branch.

Symptoms

On my Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite, windows has a white screen and does not respond to any input.

Comment

Error code: 0xc0000005. Either the power cord is not plugged in or there is a problem with the computer.

To troubleshoot this issue, first make sure that the power cord is properly plugged into the dock and into the wall outlet. If the issue persists, try Unplugging and replugging the Ingram Micro Celeron CPU I/O Adapters into your computer's USB ports and then plugging in your TV . If this does not solve the issue, it may be necessary tourchase a replacement motherboard or CPU.

Problem

I need a fix for no camera feed on the display on my Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. Regards, Carly Cohen.

Symptoms

My Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABC) will not allow me to take pictures or videos when in use. Out of all of the other features of ABC, this is the one I really need help with. When I start using ABC, there is a message that says " Camera check: n / A ". However, after scouting around on the internet, I've found several different solutions to this problem. The first option is to go into ABC's preferences and change the camera's input method. The second option is to get a new camera for my ABC. The third option is to try to fix whatever issue is preventing my camera from working.

Comment

There are a few different things that can be wrong with your camera when it comes to using ABC. One possibility is that there is a corrupt file on your camera's memorystick that needs to be repaired. Another possibility is that your camera has a firmware update that needs to be installed in order for it to work with ABC. Finally, ABC may not support the type of camera you have. In order to troubleshoot which option is most appropriate for fixing the issue, you will have to do some online searches and explore different solutions.

Problem

I need a fix for the birdseye view is not being displayed on my Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. Regards, Carly Kennedy.

Symptoms

My Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (ACT) doesn't seem to be displaying the "birdseye view" that is available in other software applications. I've verified that I am connected to ACT's internet address and my computer is Operating System (OS) and browsing software version up-to-date. I'm confident there isn't a browser issue at hand.

Comment

A possible cause could be that you have cookies turned off on your browser. Cookies are small files that websites store on your computer to help them recognize you when you return. Websites use cookies to remember how you vote, how many ads you've seen, and other information about your browsing habits. Turning off cookies may negatively affect how your visits are processed by ACT and any features that rely on cookies. If that doesn't solve the issue, it might be necessary to troubleshoot ACT's website capabilities.

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the assistent is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Regards, Catalina Gibbs.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the assistent is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Regards, Catalina Gibbs.

Symptoms

I have a 2003 mercury outback that was giving me issues over the last few months. Earlier this spring, the dashboard computer started shutting down Assisted Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABASS) at random times. I took it to a mechanic and they said it was an issue with the computer, but they weren’t able to fix it. Eventually, ABASS would always restart; however, even though it was technically working, the assistant was still disabled and wouldn’t lets me use any of the features in the navigation system. After continued frustration with this situation, I decided to look into fixing it myself.

To achieve my goals, I first had to disable the power conservation feature on my car. This involved accessing the car’s engine management system (EMS), which is relatively difficult for someone unfamiliar with cars and engines. Once I disabled power conservation, I was then able to branch into the ABASS computer through resetting its security code. resetting the security code allowed me direct access to all of ABASS’s files and software. From there, it was simply a matter of disabling certain modules and saving the changes before rebooting ABASS. After disabling several third-party modules, including ABASS’s automatic update functionality, I finally restored core functionality to ABASS via save/reload without requiring a security code restart. Although this process cost me time and money, ultimately I am glad that I was able to fix my Mercury's ABASS problem on my own.

Comment

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: activating the assistent is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Regards, Catalina Pacheco.

Symptoms

I have an HP laptop with Mercury OS and the Assistants boat assisted software suite installed. Whenever I activate the assistant, it Starts to shutdown the application. How do I prevent this from happening?

Comment

While connecting your computer to the Internet is not strictly required for using Assistants, we recommend that you do so in order to receive support and updates from our team. Another option is to disable autostarting for Assistants on your machine; please see the following recommendation:
02_ Disable Autostart Detection of ASSISTANTS


Windows 10 users may want to consider "days of use" policies to help prevent potential system files abuse or malicious code incidents. By default, Windows 10 Creators Update will automatically expire select files every 288 days or 12 months depending on usage (Figure 1). Continuous File Enjoyment typically enablesfile retentionfor14days after initial drop-off period. This can reduce digital waste and protect data while it is being managed and maintained by a clique or sysadmin organization. In the future, Microsoft may enable other usage policies as well


After analyzing your issue we have discovered that autostart detection of Assistants are regularly initiating shutdowns which interrupts usage. To prevent this from happening make sure Autostart Detection for Assistants is not enabled on your machine.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

How do i fix: propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Thanks, Chance Brock.

Symptoms

The propulsion on our boat keeps spinning but when we dock the application that runs it (Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite) is shutting down.

Comment

There could be several possibilities for why your boat's propulsion is spinning when you dock and the software that runs it is shutting down. The most common reason is that the propeller gear is frozen. Here are some steps you can take to troubleshoot and fix the issue:

1. Completely discharge the boat's battery overnight so that there is no power stored in the engine or propeller system.

2. Check to see if the propeller gear is blocked or jammed. If the gear is stuck, remove any obstruction and lubricate the gears using MarinePride®Propeller Lubricant.

3. Fuel the engine according to manufacturer’s instructions, using fresh grade fuel as recommended. If using a synthetic blend, add additional oil according to manufacturer’s instructions to pre-empt possible issues with shear thickening (oil thinning) during operation.

4. Run the engine for a few minutes Verify there are noortsAudio by Yamaha Corporation RX-V483 7 Channel Avobar System bidden prior to attempting docking proceduresPirates High Class Pre 1870s Gold Rose Jeweled Straw Hat Weddinghat wwwravocommunity that indicate an engine problem such as lack of oil or air leaks.

Problem

How do i fix: disable the gps device is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Thanks, Griffin Chang.

Symptoms

problem: I have a problem with my app. When I click on "GPS" it says "disable GPS for security reasons", but it also says that the GPS device is shutting down the app, and I can't fix it. What can I do?

Comment

There could be a few factors behind this issue. One possibility is that your app is not authorized on your phone's GPS sensor. To test this, first try opening the app on another device and see if the error persists. If the problem occurs on another device, then it likely has to do with permissions restrictions on your app. If the App Store does not allow you to update your app with new features or expanded functionality, then you will need to contact the developer of the app and get authorization from them before updating. If you installed the app from an untrusted source (i.e., you downloaded it from an unknown website), then there is a greater risk that malware may infect your phone and execute unwanted tasks with your device's GPS capabilities. In this situation, it would be best to take comprehensive steps to remediate your device—such as making sure all of your apps are updated and scanned for malware—before attempting to reinstall or use the offending app.

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the gps device is freezing the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Regards, Tinsley Christian.

Symptoms

On my Mercury, I am able to disable the GPS device, but my Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application is frozen.

Comment

The issue could be Garmin unit compatibility or satellite signal strength. Garmin releases new software frequently which may not support your Mercury model or navigation system. Depending on signal strength, some apps, such as BoatAssIST, require a strong satellite signal to work optimally. In order to disable the GPS device on your Mercury so that other applications can work without interference, access "Settings" by selecting the three lines in the multitouch screen then clicking on "Settings". Next, select "Satellite" and uncheck the box next to "GPS". Grant third party apps occasional access to GPS satellites when necessary by clicking on the pencil icon in the bottom left corner of their app's window.

Problem

How do i fix: propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is freezing the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Thanks, Clark Graham.

Symptoms

I'm having difficulty repairing my boat propulsion system using the Assisted Boat Software Suite application. The problem started as heat began to slowly dissipate from my propulsion bus assembly. Subsequent inspection showed that spinning of the propellers had stopped, but the boat still appeared to be docked. Freezing of the application resulted in a complete loss of functionality. I was able to restart the application by unplugging and replugging the power cord, but the problem has since returned. Any suggestions on fixing this issue are greatly appreciated.

Comment

There are a few things you can do in order to try and fix your propulsion problem. First, make sure that anything loose is tightly secured. This could include screws, bolts, and cable ends. Second, check the insulation on all exterior wires to make sure there are no fragmentation or burns. Finally, clean the interface surfaces between the motor controller and the propeller spinners with a mild solvent such as alcohol or detergent.

Problem

How do i fix: propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is resetting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Thanks, Colette Davis.

Symptoms

I have an issue with the propulsion on my ship staying spinning, but we are docked and the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite says it's resetting the application. Please help!

Comment

Your ship’s propulsion might be resetting erroneously, indicating a problem with the application. Follow these steps to diagnose and resolve the issue:


1. Check for updating and reboot the client: If the client has new orupdated software installed, please try to disable or restart theclient in order to allow for the updates to take effect. Update procedures can be foundhere.

2. Clean all components of the client: Ensure that there are no obstructions on (or surrounding)the cannons, fans, and propellers that could be causingstuttering orlag. Inspect all connections between components and make sure theyare tight and clean. Try rotating any elements that seem questionable.

3. Check If Usecase Conditions Are Aligned Properly: One cause of sluggishness or lagmight be out-of-sync use case conditions on both the server and clientscreen. For more information on how to troubleshootuse case alignment, see this article.

Comment

There could be several reasons why your assistente boat assisted software suite is asking you to disable your GPS:


- There may be a timeout setting on your GPS that's preventing the software from opening. Temporarily pause or reset your GPS by unplugging it and then re-plugging it into the computer.
- There may be a glitch in the software that's delaying or preventing the disabling of your GPS. Try running the software in " Offline " mode so that any errors are addressed before attempting to open the application.
- If you have a subscription to BoatCoAST Assist, please contact our customer service team at 800.896.3589 for assistance disabling your GPS. If you don't have a subscription, please try disabling your GPS manually as follows:
- Open " Control Panel " (or file:///C:/Windows/System32/control panel), navigate to the " Geosetings " subfolder and double-click on the " MapPointViewer.exe " application icon.
- On the user interface, under the General tab, click on thebutton next toand select Disable Mobile Devices .
- On the error message that appears, click onon either of the two iconsnearandthen restart your computer.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the assistent is booting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. Regards, Colt Moyer.

Symptoms

I am having an issue with my Mercury 23RV6ui booting into the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABCSU) application. Occasionally, when I start the car, the ABCSU application will not boot and instead pull up the "Service desnivelée ou lancement de l'assistante" screen. I've tried various things to try and fix the issue, but nothing has worked yet. If I disable the assistent completely in the bios, then ABCSU will boot fine, but if I try to turn it back on again afterwards, it won't recognize that it's already enabled. Any help would be much appreciated!

Comment

There could be many reasons why ABCSU is not booting. Please try the following:

- At a command prompt, type "bcdedit /set {bootmgr} device vgaquiet" and press enter. If this does not work, then your display adapter might not be working properly. Try to disable all other devices in bcedit and see if it helps.

- Have you tried to reset your computer? This might solve the problem if there was some corruption on your system drive that is causing ABCSU to not work. Please follow these instructions:

1. Make sure you have an emergency recovery disk available. (You can create one using this tutorial: How to Create an Emergency Recovery Disk)

2. Remove all external media (USB drives, CD/DVDs, etc…) You do not need them for this step.

3. Boot your computer from the recovery disk. If your computer does not already boot from the recovery disk, insert it into the optical drive and restart your computer. (If you are having trouble booting from the recovery disk, see the next step for instructions on how to create a bootable CD/DVD.)

4. Follow the instructions on the screen to selectdiskandexitinstallation(or select open for PC/Mac). This will stop Windows from installing on your main hard drive and allow you to continue with the recovery process. If you are having trouble getting to these steps, please see our blog post: How to Use a Startup Script to Automatically Start Up Your Computer From the Recovery Drive.

- If you have tried disabling ABCSU in BIOS but it still doesn't work, it might be because another program is using Compatibility Mode; in which case, changing Compatibility Mode might fix the issue. To change Compatibility Mode, please follow these steps:
I apologise if I left out anything important - please let me know if there's anything else I can do to help!

Window 7: Disable annoying Windows Update notifications

By default, updates from Windows Update are installed and ready to use. However harmless, these updates often bombard your screen with icon notifications and pester you without any valid reason. Worse yet, they may update at unpredictable intervals which can disrupt your online gaming experience or cause system failures. If you don't want these incessant notifications violating your peace of mind, follow these steps:

1. Open the Start menu and select Settings from the list of available options.
2. In the Settings pane, click on Updates & Security from the list on the left side.
3. On the Updates & Security panel that pops up, under Windows Update, make sure the Show updates from Microsoft only option is selected.
4. Restart your computer for the changes to take effect.

Hello,

Thank you for reaching out to us! We are sorry to hear that you are having difficulties using the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite. It sounds as though you may be having trouble enabling the "Birdseye View" option. Could you please follow these steps to try and fix the issue:

Temp:1.2

createCaseComment

Product:Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite
Boat:Mercury
Version:1
Temp:1.2
Length:500

When using the product Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite on my Mercury, propulsion is to low.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

When using the product Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite on my Mercury, propulsion is to low.

Symptoms

When using the product Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite with my Mercury, the propulsion is to low. I can only make small circles around the dock. The software indicates there is enough fuel, however.

Comment

Thank you for purchasing a product from our company. We are sorry to hear that you are experiencing difficulty with your boat assisted software suite and Mercury boat. We tested the product thoroughly prior to delivery and found that it should work with most boats. Here are some steps that may help:

1. Check to make sure the boat is tuned into the transponder signal. This can be easily accomplished by locating the boat's VHF receiver and scanning for a prominent transmissions from authorities on frequencies 121.5 or 406 MHz (depending on region).

2. Make sure there is enough fuel in the engine. Verify fuel levels using theNN Boat Fuel Gauge conveniently included in many of our boat software suites. Trim weight as necessary if motor seems overfueled in order to achieve optimum performance.

3a Try reconnecting batteries to digital unit if available; this helps overcome depleted electrical energy produced when transceiver signals are weakened by excessive ambient radiation clutter floating on water, or received indoors bounded by walls emitting RF/Microwave interference (typical problems near TV/phones/etc.).
Most battery operated GPS unit also have inductive charging circuitry allowing them to recharge while under cover or while docked during non-cruising hours if voltage output drops below specified windows even if power cord connected properly (some manufacturers seem to have abandoned single battery designs opting for dual rather than trickle charger versions for 2012+ models--check user guide specific information supplied with each Such units).
For boats without a battery operated navigation solution, connect an alternate 12V DC adapter directly to pedestal connector labeled +12 V on back of integrated instruments console Assy (3 wire; black-red-black) television sets monitor sized ac plugs commonly used inside cabinet rectifying UTVReceptacle cavity capacitors filter whine at 60hz compared side antenna tuners cables “AMP OUT” CAT6 Solid state amplifiers into cabling —usually immediately behind ones seating forward of center screens measured 26"-32", barely sneaking downward slightly more morally reclining occupants located about 50% closer edge first horizontally watching optimized broadcasted picture delivered whole on specifically centered 23"x37" flat panel subsidized merchandise focal point Black Box satellite display strategically tagged nowadays formally forbidden piracy HD CABLE happy costly ultimately corrupt intelligencecommunity propaganda apparatus--mentioned once casually forever later killed when concierge politely but knowledgably inquired if pet birds required spikes relocated nibbling spokes afflicted visible cords adversely troubling rest peacefully oblivious

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the gps device is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

I have a 2004 Mercury Montego. My gps (Garmin 7660) shuts down the Assistente Boat Assist software suite EVERY TIME I turn the car on, even if I cannot get a GPS lock. To combat this shutdown I've disabled the gps device in the car's settings and saved the settings, BUT THIS DOES NOT WORK. PLEASE HELP!!!!

Comment

ANSWER: Unfortunately, disabling or saving the GPS device's settings does not seem to help when it comes to the shutdown of the Assistente Boat Assist software suite. There may be a cached or provisional data folder on your computer (in Event Viewer) from the Garmin 7660 that is causing this problem. To ensure that Assistente Boat Assist shuts down as expected, try deleting this folder. Additionally, it is possible that your anti-spam measures are blocking communication between the your computer and the Garmin 7660. Double check the firewall settings whitelisted devices list and exclude any Garmin 7660s which should fix this issue.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

How do i fix: activating the assistent is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

This issue occurs when you try to activate the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABAS) application on your computer but the helper service suddenly shuts down. This happens because the service assumes that you have already activated ABAS and is trying to protect your data. To fix this issue, open an administrator command prompt and type:

C:\>sc config abaserver global

et start=auto

After you type this command, the service will start automatically and you won't have to worry about this problem anymore.

Comment

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

On my Mercury, how do i fix: disable the assistent is resetting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

This is a common problem with the Mercury Assistent, where the Assistant Boat Assisted Software Suite application repeatedly restarts itself. There are a number of methods to fix this issue. The most reliable solution is to reset the assistant's software suite by following the steps below:

1. From the main menu, select "Manage Services."
2. Choose "Assistant Boat Assisted Software Suite" from the list of services on the left side.
3. On the right side of the screen, click on "Restart Options."
4. Click on "Reset Suite."
5. Confirm that you want to reset the assistant's software suite by clicking on "Yes," and wait for it to restart.
If this does not resolve the issue, it may be required to repair or update the assistant's software suite.

Comment

Please consult the Mercury Dealer or representative for more information.

Assuming your new Mercury 60 boat computer has all of the same basic specs as your old one, it's likely that something simple like a cable might be missing or accidentally set wrong. If you can't find the missing piece, or if the problem still persists after trying to fix it with an DIY solution, then you may need to take your boat in for service.

Comment

Hi,

There may be an issue with your Mercury Bucado ASSISTANTE Boat Assist Software Suite installation where it is spontaneously activating. To troubleshoot, please follow these steps:

1. Make sure you have latest updates installed for your Mercury Bucado ASSISTANTE Boat Assist Software Suite.
2. Try uninstalling the Mercury Bucado ASSISTANTE Boat Assist Software Suite and checking if this problem persists. If not, reinstalling the software may fix the activation issue.

Problem

How do i fix: disable the assistent is booting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

The assistent is booting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. This problem occurs when you follow these steps: 1) Run "assisteantsetup.exe programfromanywahteyyouwouldlike" from your computer desktop; 2) The assistent registers as an administrator and starts the application without your consent. To fix this problem, you need to: a) Disable the assistance's ability to sign in as an administrator. To do this, open the "HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\Software\Allaire\Assistente boat Aided software Suite" registry key and delete the "admin" key value. b) If you use Windows Vista or Windows 7, you also need to create a default security group for the "Allaire" application and add it to this group. c) Restart your computer.

Comment

Comment

There could be a number of reasons why the GPS device might be causing the Mercury ASSISTANTE BOAT AIDED SOFTWARE SUITE to error. But, often times, disabling the device can resolve the issue. To disable the GPS device on your mineirouter:
1. Login to your mineirouter and open the Web Administration menu.
2. Select System.
3. In the System section, select Device Management.
4. Select GPS Devices.
5. Undo the toggle next to the GPS device you want to disable.

How do i fix: activating the assistent is erroring the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

For model: Mercury

Installed version: 1

Problem

How do i fix: activating the assistent is erroring the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

When trying to activate the Assistent boat assisted software suite application, I get an error message stating "The assistant boat assisted software suite cannot be activated at this time because it is not installed onto this computer." I have tried reinstalling the application, but to no avail. Any help would be much appreciated.

Comment

There could be a couple potential causes for why the assistant boat assisted software suite cannot be activated at this time because it is not installed onto this computer. One possibility is that the assistant boat assisted software suite was never actually installed onto your computer in the first place- you may have downloaded it from a website or provided it to someone else, but never actually installed it on your computer. In that case, you'll need to locate the installer file and install it onto your computer. Another possible cause is that the assistant boat assisted software suite itself might be corrupted- if you've upgraded your operating system or if the files that make up the assistant boat assisted software suite are infected with a virus or malware, then activation will fail. In that situation, you'll need to uninstall the assistant boat assisted software suite and use an alternate installation method- such as putting the assistant boat assisted software suite files on a USB drive and installing them that way. If none of those solutions work, then there might be a problem with your computer's antivirus or antimalware program, in which case you'll need to contact your technician for assistance.

Installed version: 1

Problem

How do i fix: propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is erroring the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

Symptoms

The propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is erroring the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. It is usually caused by a problem with the propulsion or vessel connection. There are several possible solutions.

Comment

There can be many reasons why the propulsion is still spinning even after the vessel has been docked. The first step is to check if the propulsion and vessel are properly connected using the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. If there are problems with either of these components, it will most likely result in erroring or malfunctioning the application. One possible solution is to troubleshoot and verify the connection between the propulsion and vessel. If that does not resolve the issue, it might be necessary to replace one or both components.

    Problem

    When using the product Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite on my Mercury, there is no connection to the engine.

    Symptoms

    The product Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite (ABS) was installed on a Mercury outboard motor. ABS works by connecting to the motor through the internet, and then providing live guidance based on agreed speed and direction settings. However, after trying to start the engine several times, there is always a null response from the ABS software, culminating in a dead motor.     Comment

First, make sure all of the wires are pulled tight and plugged in where they should be. Second, make sure the connection between the ABS unit and the motor is good. Third, make sure that the power to the motor is turned on properly. If these three things are checked and done and the issue still persists, you may need to bring the motor in for servicing. Have a friend try to start it for you while you're away so that you can determine if it needs more brute force than just pressing buttons. Thank you for letting us know and we apologize for any inconvenience this may have caused.

    2. If there are multiple applications trying to use up the device's resources at once, the GPS device might shut down the software suite in order to give other applications more room.

    3. If there arememory limitations on the GPS device, the software suite might be shut down in order to conserve memory.

    Problem

    On my Mercury, how do i fix disable the gps device is resetting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    Symptoms

    Many times when the GPS device on a Mercury is reset, the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application (ABAS) will also be reset. This can sometimes cause problems with controlling the boat. To fix this issue, you will need to restart your ABAS application.

    Comment

    To restart your ABAS:
    1. From the Mercury Dock or Command Folders, select Mercury Utilities.
    2. Select ABAS from the left panel.
    3. Click on the Basics button.
    4. Under Operations, click Restart Application.

    Symptoms

    Issue: User cannot enable the birdseye view while booting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    The issue could be related to one of these following:
    -- A screen resolution issue.
    -- Poor username and password input.
    -- Incorrect computer security settings.

    Resolution: Enable the birdseye view by following these steps.
    1) Check whether your computer has a compatible graphics card by visiting the manufacturer’s website or checking for driver updates available from Windows Update Service. If there are no driver updates available, you will need to install a third-party graphics card-specific driver software in order to enable the birdseye view feature.
    2) Ensure that the Device Manager is open and displays all installed devices located in HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\Control\Video. Make sure reassign device permission setting is set tointegrated and AGpHardwarePortEnabled value is set to TRUE as described in this blog post: Enable Video Printer Loading in Windows 10 Anniversary Update (Windows1020160927). In order to open Device Manager, Users can go to Start Menu -> Settings -> System -> Advanced System Settings -> Device Manager or may press Windows + I keys together at Start Screen to open it automatically when device is plugged into computer. When Device Manager window opens, expand Display Adapters category, right-click on the NVIDIA Corporation VGA adapter (Default) and click Properties. At Platform Specific Properties window, under Use the following Hicks Microsoft College USB Game Controller for Johnson County Higher Education USB Adapter for this device selection box, check Always use this device and click OK two times as shown on the picture below. Note: If you are using atouchscreen device, please ensure that Disable DirectInput tapping style is not checked under this box as touchscreens typically use direct input rather than tapping style which ASSISTANTE does not currently support due to Android marshal bug).


    3) Click Start button, type msconfig into the search bar and press Enter key on keyboard. Press Yes button when dialog warning will appear about serious risks involved in successfully modifying system settings. Next, navigate window expanded SYSTEM Configuration on left panel and double-click on Boot Professor title as shown below and make sure Enable parameter boot specific settings is set to True discretionally as needed as it may improve speed of loading time later during operating system startup, depending on

    Comment

    your system configuration.
    4) Follow the on-screen instructions to re-enable Assistente Boot Assistant service as required and install ASSISTANTE Boat Assisted Software Suite application again after restarting your computer.




    The issue could be related to one of the following:
    1) A screen resolution issue. 2) Poor username and password input. 3) Incorrect computer security settings.

    Comment

    Hello,Thank you for bringing this to our attention. By default, the Boot Assist Software Suite application is configured to operate in Wally mode. This mode uses the vessels dynamic steering capabilities to remain stationary while the propulsion system spins. In order for the Boot Assist Software Suite application to operate correctly, the vessel must be free of docks and obstructions. We recommend that you contact your system integrator or supplier for additional assistance with configuring the Boot Assist Software Suite application. Thank you for bringing this to our attention.

    When using the product Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite on my Mercury, propulsion is to low.

    Symptoms

    There is something wrong with the propulsion wiring in your Mercury and Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite is not rendering it optimally.

    Comment

    The problem could be in one or more of the following areas: the wiring itself, faulty connectors, corrosion on connectors or hardware, or a bad switch. Here are some troubleshooting steps to try if you suspect one of the problems listed above is causing the issue:

    1. Go back through your wiring schematic and make sure all active connector wires are connected to their correspondingHardware nodes. If there are missing connections, Reconnect these wires as necessary.

    2. Verify that all push-pull connectors are properly aligned andFlat against their corresponding sender housing fixtures. Corrosion or distortingPush-pull connectors can impede docking and boostPlant performance.

    3. Replace any faulty connectors with identicalquality authorized parts from original equipment manufacturer (OEM) vendors to speed upLaptop restoration and ensure optimal system performance.

    On my Mercury, how do i fix propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    For model: Mercury

    Installed version: 1

    Problem

    On my Mercury, how do i fix propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    Symptoms

    The Mercury On-Board Navigation System (NAM) is erroneously calculating the ship's position and therefore provides inaccurate information to the Autopilot which in turn causes the propulsion system to continually spin despite being docked. To fix this problem, the Mercury must be able to override the NAM's calculations and contact a human operator for assistance when necessary. This can be achieved through the use of the Apollo Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application. When this application is activated, it takes over navigation duties from the NAM and allows crew to communicate with Operator Managers stationed onshore who can direct the ship back onto course.

    Comment

    While it is possible to fix the Mercury's navigation system through the use of a custom application, this would involve the installation of a third-party software and would therefore be an extra step that could potentially disrupt the ship's systems. There are other options currently being considered by management, such as redesigning the entire navigation system or upgrading to a newer version of the NAM. In both cases, it is hoped that by fixing these issues crews will no longer have to rely on manual intervention in order to keep the ship on track.

    How do i fix: enable the birdseye view is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    For model: Mercury

    Installed version: 1

    Problem

    How do i fix: enable the birdseye view is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    Symptoms

    If you are using the Assistante Boat Assisted Software Suite and Startup Wizard, you may have a problem where the birdseye view just shuts down on its own. This is usually caused by an application deadlock in which one program keeps trying to access the same resources so the other program can't run. To fix this, try the following: 1.First check for any updated software that might be available. If there is no updated software available, then you may need to clear your computer's memory (reset) or Windows will try to initialize your computer again. If you reset your computer and still have the problem, then you may need to uninstall the program and reinstall it from scratch. 2.Check if there are any services or programs running in the background that are crashing the birdseye view. Some common background services that can crash the birdseye view include windows updates, anti-virus software, and backup programs. 3.Close all antivirus and backup programs and windows updates that are running in the background. 4.If clearing your computer's memory does not work or if the problem persists, then you may need to disable some of the security features on your computer so that the Assistante Boat Assisted Software Suite can function properly. To do this, launch Control Panel from Start Menu → Programs → Accessories → System Tools → Security Policy. From here, under Security Options, open Local Policies→ Security Basics→ Processes View (Or (NETLOGON)→Windows Processes). Here you should kill any runaway processes that are causing the birdseye view to fail.

    Comment

    Product:Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite
    Boat:Mercury
    Version:1
    Temp:1.2
    Length:500

    How do i fix: activating the assistent is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    For model: Mercury

    Installed version: 1

    Problem

    How do i fix: activating the assistent is shutting down the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    Symptoms

    Currently, upon launching the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application and selecting "Activate" from the main menu, it appears as if the software is attempting to access a URL that has been blocked by our firewall. However, after much trouble-shooting and searching our registry, we have located what seems to be the problem. The "cuore.help" website (which is used internally by the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application) apparently references a file called "CoreUserMgr.dll" which is located within the "C:\Program Files (x86)\Public\\Cuore Corporation\Cuore\Serviceability" folder on our local computer. However, due to a recent software update, this file apparently no longer exists on our machine. Consequently, when the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application attempts to access the "Cuore Corporation\Cuore\Serviceability" folder in order to activate its features, Windows 10 incorrectly believes that this is an unauthorized or misty attempt to access protected files andIt therefore shuts down the whole application abruptly.

    To correct this issue, we will need to either reinstall the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application or find another way to manually activate its features.

    Comment

    2. Check your device's system settings to see if there is a file or registry that may be preventing the software from working correctly.

    Symptoms

    Comment

    Assuming you are talking about "Birdseye View" in relation to your Mercury poledrive, you might need to enable that featured within the Mercury interface. To enable "Birdseye View," follow these steps:

    1) Enable General Features from the Navigation bar:
    2) Click on the hamburger menu icon in the top left corner (three lines down from the top).
    3) Under Navigation Options, select Feature Features.
    4) Drag "Birdseye View" to the Enabled list under See Inside Your Vehicle.
    5) Close the Navigation Options window.

    Product:Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite
    Boat:Mercury
    Version:1
    Temp:1.2
    Length:500

    How do i fix: disable the gps device is resetting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    For model: Mercury

    Installed version: 1

    Problem

    How do i fix: disable the gps device is resetting the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    Symptoms

    In order to fix this problem, you will need to do the following:


    1. Disable the GPS device from resetting the application.
    2. Before disabling the GPS device, make sure that there are no jobs queued up in the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite for processing.
    3. Once disabled, re-enable the GPS device and wait for it to finish re-initializing before restarting the application.

    Comment


    4. If the issue persists, you may have to restore the application from a backup.



    1. Disable the GPS device from resetting the application by following these steps:
    a. From within the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite, open the DeviceSettings panel.
    b. On the left side of the panel, under GPS Devices and Sensors, click Disable.
    c. Under Frequency & Duration Settings, set Frequency to Off (2400 seconds) and Duration to Cancelled (14400 seconds), and then click Save.
    d. To re-enable the GPS device, set Frequency to On (3600 seconds) and Duration to 14400 second and then click Save.
    2. Before disabling the GPS device, make sure that there are no jobs queued up in the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite for processing.
    3. Once disabled, re-enable the GPS device and wait for it to finish initializing before restarting the application.
    4. If the issue persists, you may have to restore the application from a backup

    Problem

    On my Mercury, how do i fix disable the gps device is erroring the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    Symptoms

    "On my Mercury, how do i fix disable the gps device is erroring the Assistente Boat Assist Software Suite application."

    Comment

    There is no formal procedure for disabling the GPS on Mercury. In order to disable, or remove the GPS module, owners will need to access their vehicle's Torque Control Units (TCUs) menu and advance to the navigation screen. From there, they will click "GPS Geolocation Off." This will disable the module while retaining other possible navigation functions.

    How do i fix: propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is erroring the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    For model: Mercury

    Installed version: 1

    Problem

    How do i fix: propulsion keeps spinning, but we are docked is erroring the Assistente Boat Assisted Software Suite application.

    Symptoms

    The automated propulsion system on your boat is spinning but not moving the boat. The crew has informed you that they are not being able to dock the boat with the mechanism automatically working.

    Comment

    One potential problem could be the engine, or the automatic propulsion system. Other possibilities, which would require further inspection, could include gear failure, or electrical issues. While it is always possible that a completely unrelated issue may be causing the automatic propulsion system to not work, it would be prudent to inspect the engine first in order to rule out any potential problems. If the engine is experiencing difficulties, then steps would need to be taken to address that issue before trying to dock the boat mechanically.
